
# 🚀 शानदार GPT Image 2 प्रॉम्पट्स

[![Awesome](https://awesome.re/badge.svg)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome)
[![License: CC BY 4.0](https://img.shields.io/badge/License-CC%20BY%204.0-lightgrey.svg)](https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/)
[![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts?style=social)](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)
[![PRs Welcome](https://img.shields.io/badge/PRs-welcome-brightgreen.svg)](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md)
[![Prompts](https://img.shields.io/badge/prompts-1100%2B-blue.svg)](https://www.atlascloud.ai/prompts-hub/gpt-image-2-prompt?utm_source=github&utm_campaign=awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)

> 🎨 OpenAI GPT Image 2 के लिए रचनात्मक प्रॉम्पट्स का संग्रह — with **real previews generated via Atlas Cloud**.

> ⚠️ **कॉपीराइट सूचना**: सभी प्रॉम्पट्स शैक्षिक उद्देश्यों के लिए समुदाय से एकत्र किए गए हैं। यदि आपको लगता है कि कोई सामग्री आपके अधिकारों का उल्लंघन करती है, तो कृपया [एक समस्या खोलें](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts/issues/new?template=bug-report.yml) और हम इसे तुरंत हटा देंगे।

### 🧩 Supported Models

- 🎬 **Video** — Seedance 2.0 · Kling 3 · Sora 2 · Veo 3.1 · HappyHorse 1 · Grok Imagine 1.5 · Wan 2.7
- 🎨 **Image** — Nano Banana 2/Pro · GPT Image 2 · Flux 2 · Seedream 5
- 💬 **LLM** — Claude · GPT · DeepSeek · MiniMax · Kimi · GLM · Qwen
- 🔊 **Audio** — Grok TTS
- 📚 **Explore more** — [300+ models »](https://www.atlascloud.ai/models?utm_source=github&utm_campaign=awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)

**▶ Run any prompt via Atlas Cloud**

- 🧠 **Skill (recommended)** — install [atlas-cloud-skills](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/atlas-cloud-skills) in Claude Code / Codex / Gemini CLI, then ask: *"Generate this with GPT Image 2 on Atlas Cloud: &lt;paste a prompt&gt;"*.
- 💻 **CLI** — prefer the terminal? Use [atlascloud-cli](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/cli).
- 🔑 **[Get a free API key →](https://www.atlascloud.ai/console/api-keys?utm_source=github&utm_campaign=awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)** · 300+ models, one key.

## 🤔 GPT Image 2 क्या है?

**GPT Image 2** (codename **"duct-tape"**) is OpenAI's next-generation image model. Community testing highlights a leap in these areas:

- 🎯 **Pixel-Perfect Text Rendering** — Native-quality text in Chinese, English, and Japanese, no typos or warped glyphs
- 🎨 **Cross-Image Consistency** — The same character, style, or IP stays identical across a series, down to the pixel
- ⚡ **Commercial-Grade Illustration** — Illustration output is ready to ship without manual polish
- 🌈 **True Art Style Induction** — Creatively evokes the feeling of a style rather than merely approximating references
- 🔧 **Storyboard & Product Series** — Ideal for storyboards, IP characters, and multi-panel product visuals
- 📐 **Multi-Language Design** — Social cards, banners, and posters with accurate multilingual typography in one shot

📚 **Learn More:** See community testing in our [report summary](docs/FAQ.md)

### 🚀 Raycast एकीकरण

कुछ प्रॉम्पट्स [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) सिंटैक्स का उपयोग करके **गतिशील तर्क** का समर्थन करते हैं। 🚀 Raycast Friendly बैज देखें!

**उदाहरण:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

Raycast में उपयोग करते समय, आप त्वरित पुनरावृत्ति के लिए तर्कों को गतिशील रूप से प्रतिस्थापित कर सकते हैं!

## 🔥 विशेष प्रॉम्पट्स

> ⭐ असाधारण गुणवत्ता और रचनात्मकता के लिए हमारी टीम द्वारा हाथ से चुना गया

### No. 1: हार्दिक 4-पैनल विवाहित जोड़े का मंगा

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट एक विवाहित जोड़े का जश्न मनाते हुए एक नरम, रोमांटिक चार-पैनल जापानी कॉमिक उत्पन्न करता है, जो सोशल पोस्ट्स, स्मारकीय चित्रण, या रिश्ता-थीम वाले मंगा आर्ट के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
{"type":"4-panel romantic manga illustration","style":"clean hand-drawn anime line art with a warm beige and light brown monochrome palette, soft cream background, simple shading, cozy and gentle atmosphere, social media post aesthetic","format":"square 2x2 comic layout with thin brown panel borders","headline":{"text":"{argument name=\"headline text\" default=\"夫婦の日\"}","position":"top center","decorations":{"count":2,"items":["small heart on the left","small heart on the right"]}},"panels":[{"panel":1,"count":2,"scene":"standing portrait of a young couple","composition":"the man ### No. 2: प्यारा ब्लैक किटन जापानी स्टिकर शीट

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 विवरण

A candid, photorealistic vertical smartphone photo of a young East Asian woman standing in a warm-toned boutique or home fragrance shop, shot from a slightly high angle looking down at her upper body and torso. She wears a very fitted ribbed zip-front long-sleeve top in {argument name="outfit color" default="chocolate brown"}, partially unzipped, paired with matching high-waisted pants in the same brown tone for a monochrome look. Her pose is casual and slightly leaning, with the other arm relaxed behind her back, giving the image an off-guard lifestyle snapshot feeling. The store shelves around her are wooden and filled with many glass candle jars and small product containers, softly blurred in the background and along the left side of the frame. Use warm indoor ambient lighting, shallow depth of field, realistic skin texture, subtle highlights on the hair, natural hand pose, and a cozy artisanal retail atmosphere. Compose it as a tight mid-to-full body crop in portrait orientation, with the subject centered and the background angled diagonally to enhance the candid perspective. Photographic style: realistic, high-detail, soft bokeh, boutique shopping snapshot, 35mm lens look, natural color grading.
```

### No. 5: साइबरपंक रूफटॉप ब्रीच रेड

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट बारिश वाली नीयन-रोशनी वाली छत पर एक दरवाजे को तोड़ते हुए पांच-सदस्यीय सामरिक टीम का नाटकीय विस्तृत साइबरपंक एक्शन दृश्य बनाता है, जो डायस्टोपियन साइ-फाई कॉन्सेप्ट आर्ट या सिनेमाई गेम विज़ुअल्स के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A cinematic cyberpunk night raid on a rain-soaked rooftop balcony in a dense futuristic megacity, viewed in a wide-angle shot from slightly behind and to the side of the squad. Five heavily armed tactical soldiers in black futuristic body armor and full helmets stack at a metal door on the far left: 1 soldier is actively breaching the door with one boot raised and bright orange sparks exploding outward, 1 soldier stands just behind aiming into the doorway, 1 soldier crouches low in the center with rifle ready, 1 soldier stands mid-right aiming across the balcony toward the city, and 1 soldier kneels in the right foreground behind the railing. The environment is packed with towering skyscrapers, elevated skybridges, distant traffic lanes, wet reflective metal surfaces, drifting steam, rain haze, and a deep blue-black stormy sky. Neon signage and giant billboards dominate the scene in magenta, cyan, violet, and electric blue, including visible signs reading "POCARI SWEAT" twice, "softsys", "DATA INC", "ROSE", "BARIKI", "2F", "KIROSHI", and multiple vertical Japanese and Chinese-style neon signs. Include 2 hovering flying vehicles in the mid-distance sky and countless illuminated windows receding into the background. The overall mood should feel gritty, moody, high-contrast, and slightly glitchy, with nostalgic old-school AI-art instability: some billboard portraits are malformed or partially censored by soft purple rectangular blocks, a few signs feel inconsistent, and fine architectural details subtly smear or repeat. Emphasize wet reflections, volumetric fog, sparks, rim lighting on the soldiers, dense urban depth, and a dramatic action-movie composition in the style of a dystopian sci-fi concept art keyframe.
```

### No. 3: किराना गलियारा अंडे के डिब्बे पोर्ट्रेट

![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट किराने की दुकान में एक स्टाइलिश महिला का एक यथार्थवादी ऊर्ध्वाधर लाइफस्टाइल फोटो उत्पन्न करता है जो अंडों के छह के खुले डिब्बे को पकड़े हुए है, जो सोशल मीडिया या संपादकीय-शैली की शॉपिंग इमेजरी के लिए उपयुक्त है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A candid vertical smartphone photo of a {argument name="woman age" default="young adult"} woman shopping in a modern grocery store aisle at night, framed from upper thighs to head in a close, slightly wide-angle perspective. She is standing beside refrigerated produce shelves filled with colorful packaged vegetables and groceries, with glossy black shelving, bright store lighting, reflective surfaces, and soft bokeh in the background. She holds an open recycled cardboard egg carton toward the camera in her left hand, clearly showing 6 brown eggs inside. Her right hand is near a black shopping basket cart filled with groceries. She has long dark brown hair worn down, and her face is intentionally obscured by a large soft-edged rectangular blur block centered over the face. She wears a tight ribbed brown zip-front long-sleeve crop top with the zipper partly open at the chest, and matching high-waisted brown pants. The pose is casual and confident, with the carton presented as the focal prop. Realistic photography, flashless indoor lighting, shallow depth of field, detailed skin and fabric texture, natural reflections, high contrast, fashionable lifestyle aesthetic, subtle editorial feel, vertical 9:16 composition.
```

### No. 10: महाकाव्य नॉर्स आकाश योद्धा क्रिस्टल जानवरों के साथ

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट एक नाटकीय लंबवत फंतासी-एनीमे स्प्लैश चित्र बनाता है, जिसमें एक सींग वाला आकाश योद्धा और तीन क्रिस्टल-कवच वाले पशु साथी हैं, जो पोस्टर, कार्ड आर्ट, या गेम की विजुअल्स के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A dynamic high-fantasy anime illustration in a vertical poster composition, showing 4 heroic figures suspended in a stormy celestial sky filled with glowing clouds, blue crystal shards, and floating turquoise feathers. At the center, a tall armored male warrior inspired by a Norse god stands as the commanding focal point, with long flowing brown hair, a gold-and-teal horned helmet, a dark green and blue cape whipping in the wind, ornate black, teal, and gold armor with an open muscular chest, and a bright cyan wolf emblem glowing on his chest. He raises one hand upward toward a radiant circular magical sigil above him, while his other hand holds a long spear with a crystalline blue spearhead. Around him are 3 fox-and-wolf-like companion creatures in matching ice-crystal armor. In the lower foreground, 1 large ferocious orange wolf charges toward the viewer with its mouth open in a roar, oversized claws extended, white mane, blue crystal head armor, blue-and-gold armor plates on its back and legs, and a huge fluffy tail. On the upper left, 1 athletic orange fox warrior leaps forward midair wearing angular blue crystal armor and large faceted blue wings, posed like a fast aerial attacker. On the right, 1 small cute chibi fox companion floats happily with big blue eyes, a wide smile, a blue tunic-like outfit with glowing cyan patterns, and a crystal crown on its head. Use vivid saturated colors, especially electric cyan, sapphire blue, teal, gold, and orange. The mood is epic, divine, and magical, with strong motion lines, dramatic foreshortening, glowing highlights, detailed fur and feathers, polished crystal textures, and cinematic fantasy trading-card splash art quality.
```

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

एक हास्यपूर्ण भू-राजनीतिक मीम चित्रण जो संयुक्त राज्य अमेरिका और ईरान के कंट्रीबॉल को होर्मुज जलडमरूमध्य में एक-दूसरे का सामना करते हुए दिखाता है, जो संपादकीय व्यंग्य या सोशल मीडिया टिप्पणी के लिए आदर्श है।

```
A detailed satirical countryball meme illustration of the {argument name="waterway name" default="Strait of Hormuz"} as a very narrow sea passage between two steep rocky cliffs, painted in a polished digital cartoon style with dramatic shading and textured stone. In the center foreground, exactly 2 countryballs block each other in the tight channel so that only one can pass. On the left is a USA countryball with angry narrowed eyes, painted with the American flag, wearing a dark navy baseball cap labeled "USA" in large white letters. On the right is an Iran countryball with angry narrowed eyes, painted with the Iranian flag and emblem, wearing a green-and-white headband tied on the side; the headband contains Korean text that reads "저항은 우리의 권리". Above each ball is exactly 1 white speech bubble with thick black outline, for a total of 2 speech bubbles, and both say {argument name="speech text" default="길!"} in large bold Korean lettering, as if neither side will yield. Show the two balls facing each other nose-to-nose in a standoff in the bottleneck. On the left cliff, include exactly 1 wooden sign reading in Korean and English: "호르무즈 해협" and "Strait of Hormuz". On the right cliff, include exactly 1 warning sign with Persian text at the top and a red warning triangle below, indicating that only one person can pass. In the left bottom corner, place exactly 1 black oil barrel labeled "OIL" with dark spilled oil pooling around it. In the right bottom corner, place exactly 1 black naval mine with Persian writing on it, attached to a chain. In the background beyond the narrow passage, show open sea with exactly 3 distant ships, including at least 1 larger tanker and faint dark smoke rising into the sky. Use a tense but humorous geopolitical meme tone, centered composition, eye-level view, soft daylight, slightly muted realistic colors, crisp outlines, and high readability for all text.
```

### No. 17: एनिमे पॉप-आर्ट प्रदर्शन पोस्टर

```
A bold Korean beverage advertisement poster in a glossy commercial photography style, featuring {argument name="spokesperson" default="Donald Trump lookalike"} in a dark navy business suit, white dress shirt, and vivid blue tie, standing front-facing against a saturated bright-blue sky with a few soft white clouds and a faint modern city skyline including a tall skyscraper resembling the Empire State Building on the right. He is holding a cold plastic bottle of {argument name="product name" default="POCARI SWEAT"} dramatically toward the camera in his left hand, with extreme foreshortening so the bottle appears large in the foreground and the person is slightly behind it. The bottle is clear with condensation, a white cap, visible water inside, and a deep blue label reading “POCARI SWEAT” in large white letters with smaller text above saying “ION SUPPLY DRINK.” Add energetic frozen water splashes and droplets around the bottle, hand, and lower foreground to emphasize freshness and hydration. Place the brand logo in the upper left corner: “POCARI SWEAT” in white with the curved underline mark. Across the top, add huge distressed white Korean headline text, slightly angled and filling most of the upper half: {argument name="headline text" default="갈증 해소? 이걸로 끝! 포카리스웨트!"}. In the lower right over the suit, add a bold italic quotation in white and blue Korean text: {argument name="quote" default="WINNING은 수분 싸움! 포카리스웨트로 리프레시!"}. In the bottom left, include exactly 3 circular benefit icons stacked vertically with short Korean labels: a water drop icon with “수분 보충”, a lightning bolt icon with “전해질 보충”, and a running figure icon with “빠른 흡수”. Use a high-contrast, patriotic blue-and-white color palette, dramatic ad lighting, sharp focus on the bottle and hand, slightly softer focus on the face and background, and an overall energetic premium campaign-poster look.
```

### No. 26: कोरियन राइस ड्रिंक पैरोडी विज्ञापन पोस्टर

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट एक मज़ाकिया, उच्च-प्रभाव वाला पैरोडी पेय विज्ञापन पोस्टर बनाता है, जिसमें एक कोरियन कैन्ड राइस ड्रिंक को प्रमोट करते हुए एक प्रसिद्ध राजनीतिज्ञ-जैसे प्रवक्ता को दिखाया गया है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
Create a bold Korean-style beverage advertisement poster with a warm golden splash background and dramatic commercial lighting. Show a {argument name="celebrity spokesperson" default="Donald Trump-like older male politician"} from the chest up, wearing a navy suit, white dress shirt, bright red tie, and a small American flag lapel pin, facing camera with a confident sales-pitch expression. His face is obscured by a flat rectangular censor block in a skin-toned color. In his left hand, extended close to the camera in forced perspective, he holds a yellow aluminum can of Korean rice punch drink labeled prominently in Korean, with red top and bottom bands and the main product text "비락 식혜" and "Since 1993" on the can. The can also includes smaller Korean copy, an image of sweet rice drink near the bottom, and the volume text "238 ml (120 kcal)". His right hand gives a thumbs-up.

Use an energetic retro-commercial composition, with splashing sweet rice beverage and droplets behind him, glowing golden highlights, and a slightly low-angle heroic framing. At the top, include 3 distinct headline text groups: a small handwritten-style black slogan on the upper left reading "전통의 맛, 한국의 DRINK!", a huge central headline in distressed bold Korean type reading "걸죽는 땐?" in dark brown-black and "비락 식혜!" in vivid red, and a brand logo on the upper right reading "비락" with small red text "Since 1993" beneath it. Add 2 callout badges: on the left, a yellow circular seal with a tiny crown icon and the text "대한민국 국민음료 No.1"; on the right, a white speech bubble with handwritten Korean text "한국이 만든 맛있는 전통!" and red English text "I LOVE IT!".

At the bottom foreground, place 2 food elements: a brass bowl filled with sweet rice drink and floating rice grains on the left, and a wooden bowl piled with white rice on the right. Across the lower middle, add 2 lines of large brush-style promotional text, the first in white reading "달콤하게! 시원하게!" and the second in mixed white and yellow reading "속까지 시~원하게!" with an energetic yellow underline stroke. Along the very bottom, include 3 circular feature icons with captions in Korean: "국내산 쌀 엄선된 재료", "시원하게 갈증해소", and "부드러운 단맛 속 편한 식혜". In the lower right corner, add tiny disclaimer text "연출된 이미지입니다". Make the overall look glossy, exaggerated, funny, and convincing like a viral parody print ad.
```

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A hyper-detailed Japanese parody theme park advertisement poster in a vertical format, designed like a dramatic summer travel ad mixed with a luxury attraction campaign. The setting is a tropical jungle under a vivid blue sky with scattered clouds and a bright blazing sun in the upper right corner, with palm leaves framing the top edges. Across the top, place a huge 3D stone-textured Japanese headline reading {argument name="headline text" default="ジャンキリア沖縄"}, with a smaller white Japanese tagline underneath that reads "— やんばるの大自然に包まれた、超本格ジャングル・テーマパーク —". In the center, feature a large modern smartphone standing upright and slightly tilted, dominating the composition. On its screen, show a beige ticket-lottery waiting interface with jungle silhouettes at the top and large bold Japanese text reading "整理券抽選中", a circular loading indicator, and smaller text near the bottom reading "結果発表まで30分" and "※この画面を閉じずにお待ちください". The phone status bar should show 10:00. Behind the phone on the left, place a roaring Tyrannosaurus rex emerging from jungle foliage, mouth open wide, realistic and threatening. On the right, place an ornate golden entrance gate with detailed carvings and a sign reading "プレミアムパス入口", leading to a red-carpeted premium entry lane. In the foreground and midground, show a long crowded queue of park visitors stretching deep into the scene, all wearing casual summer clothing, hats, towels, backpacks, and carrying umbrellas, fans, and water bottles, suggesting extreme heat and exhaustion. Several people nearest the viewer should have blurred faces. On the far left, add a giant weathered stone sign with huge red Japanese text reading "待ち時間 180分". At the lower left, include 3 stacked rustic wooden signboards: the top sign has a blue parking icon and text "駐車場 2,000円"; the middle sign has a smartphone icon and text "アプリ必須 ダウンロードしてね!"; the bottom sign has a dinosaur silhouette and text "当選者だけが冒険へ". Near the bottom right, include 3 small circular icon callouts with short Japanese promotional lines: "抽選に選ばれし者だけが、恐竜に会える。", "スマホの充電が尽きる前に、夢は始まる。", and "プレミアムな近道も、ご用意しました。" with icons suggesting dinosaur, phone battery, and VIP access. At the very bottom center, add a black disclaimer strip with small white Japanese text reading "このポスターは架空のパロディ広告です". The overall style should be ultra-realistic, cinematic, high-contrast, satirical, and polished like a premium commercial poster, with exaggerated theme park hype, oppressive heat, and absurd queue-based adventure as the core joke.

### No. 31: जीवित पृथ्वी के बगल में अंतरिक्ष यात्री

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट एक जड़ों से ढकी पृथ्वी के बगल में तैरते एक अकेले अंतरिक्ष यात्री की एक मूडी सिनेमाई साइ-फाई छवि उत्पन्न करता है, जो सररियल स्पेस आर्ट या एआई-थीम वाली संपादकीय विजुअल्स के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

Step 1 is labeled “1 밥 간하기” and shows a bowl of rice with sesame oil and salt beside it, caption “밥에 참기름 소금으로 간하기”. ```

# Instructions
Create a minimalist theater-style vertical poster for {argument name="user input" default="[user input]"} using monochrome + {argument name="accent color" default="one accent color"}.

# Layout Requirements
- Place the title largely in the bottom 1/4 area, with the Japanese title at maximum size and the English subtitle small directly underneath.
- Place a catchphrase (1-2 lines) in the top center.
- Stack 3-4 awards/official certification badges vertically in the top-left corner.
- Place a vertical catchphrase (2-3 lines) along the right edge.
- Position the main character as a silhouette from behind, slightly left of the center.
- Represent fantastical elements (floating islands, giant creatures) in the background as silhouettes.
- Place staff credits, release date, and distribution info in a small horizontal line at the bottom.
- Highlight the release date in a large font at the bottom right.

# Design Requirements
- Keep the background monochrome (black to gray gradient).
- Use only one accent color (e.g., vivid cobalt blue or gold).
- Combine silhouette and thin line art styles.
- Emphasize the title text with white + the accent color.
- Create a cinematic and artistic atmosphere overall.
- Avoid colorful backgrounds, excessive decoration, or heavy use of gradients.
- Format: Vertical, aspect ratio 2:3, high resolution.
```

### No. 51: चार-पैनल रोमांटिक कॉमेडी मंगा पेज

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट जापानी संवाद के साथ एक मोनोक्रोम चार-पैनल मंगा पेज उत्पन्न करता है, जो अभिव्यंजक चरित्र अभिनय के साथ नाटकीय रोमांटिक-कॉमेडी बहस दृश्य बनाने के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
Create a black-and-white manga page with 4 stacked horizontal panels, clean black gutters, screentone shading, dramatic speed lines, and polished seinen-style linework. The page features two youthful anime characters with modern casual clothing and short dark hair, with the face area of both characters obscured by a soft square blur censor block. Panel 1: a slim young person with messy short dark hair and a collared shirt clenches one fist near their chest, body angled left, surrounded by an intense fiery aura effect in the background, looking emotional and defensive. On the right side, place a large jagged vertical speech balloon containing this Japanese text: 「何十時間も魂を削って描いた一枚と、プロンプト打ち込んで数秒で出した画像が同じ価値なわけないでしょ！ふざけないで！」. Panel 2: a second young person with slightly taller build, short dark hair, a dark zip jacket over a light shirt, raises one index finger calmly as if explaining a point. Add a rounded rectangular speech box on the right with this Japanese text: 「投下した労働時間で価値が決まるという典型的な“労働価値説の誤謬”だ。市場における価値は、出力された結果を受け手がどう評価するかで決まる」. Panel 3: the taller character gently pats the shorter character on the head; include a small hand-pat sound effect near the hand reading 「ポン」. The shorter character looks up in surprise. On the right side, add a large oval vertical speech balloon with this Japanese text: 「でも俺の市場価値基準はすごくシンプルだよ。君が俺のために照れてくれるこの数秒間に、何十時間分の価値も感じてるから」. Panel 4: close-up of the shorter character blushing intensely with spiral eyes, sweat drops, trembling expression, open mouth, and dense hatching on the cheeks, overwhelmed with embarrassment. Fill the background with dramatic radiating speed lines. Add a large jagged vertical speech balloon on the right with this Japanese text: 「だ、誰がアンタのために照れるか…っ！自意識過剰よ！」. Add two sound effects: a small 「プル…」 near the shoulder and a larger shaky handwritten 「カァァァ」 along the lower left side. Keep the whole page monochrome, highly expressive, romantic-comedy manga tone, with strong emotional contrast between heated argument, cool explanation, teasing affection, and flustered payoff.
```

The setting is a moody ocean cliff highway overlook with dark rocky mountains running along the left side, pale gray sea stretching into the distance on the right, and a cloudy washed-out sky. Include 1 parked light-colored late-1980s or early-1990s sedan on the right edge of the frame, rear end facing the viewer, and 1 large rock barrier near the overlook. The asphalt is dark and damp with faint parking lines, suggesting recent rain. Use natural light, muted cool tones, slight film grain, soft focus, shallow haze, and a nostalgic 35mm road-trip photography aesthetic.

### No. 53: लक्ज़री फैशन बुक स्प्रेड

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट एक खुली फैशन बुक का यथार्थवादी ओवरहेड फोटो बनाता है, जिसमें एक दो-पेज कूतुर संपादकीय स्प्रेड है, जो लक्ज़री ब्रांडिंग, मैगज़ीन मॉकअप, या स्टाइल कैंपेन विजुअल्स के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A high-end editorial fashion photograph shown as an open large-format hardcover magazine or art book lying flat on a clean off-white surface, viewed from directly above. The two-page spread contains 2 full-page portraits of the same elegant woman with her face obscured by a soft square blur, creating a privacy-censored look. On the left page, she stands against a pale stone or concrete architectural wall wearing a structured long-sleeve dress in {argument name="dress color" default="soft slate gray"}, with a fitted bodice, round neckline, sharply tailored seams, and an exaggerated sculptural bell-shaped skirt; the camera angle is slightly low, making her neck appear long and her posture statuesque. On the right page, she is photographed from the back in a dramatic {argument name="second dress color" default="black"} evening gown with a very deep open back, wide shoulder straps, and a voluminous full skirt, standing in front of a classic paneled wall or door in a dim, moody interior. Use luxury fashion magazine styling, minimal composition, muted tones, soft natural-looking light, refined shadows, realistic paper texture, visible book gutter, slightly curved pages, and crisp print detail. The overall mood is sophisticated, couture, cinematic, and understated, like a premium fashion editorial spread.
```

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://static.atlascloud.ai/prompt/gpt-image2/images/14676_1.jpg" width="600" alt="लक्ज़री फैशन बुक स्प्रेड - Image 1">

```
A candid documentary-style photo of a {argument name="setting" default="high school computer lab classroom"} filled with exactly 10 students seated at rows of bulky off-white CRT desktop computers, viewed from the back-left corner of the room at a slight wide angle. In the foreground left, a student in a navy track jacket with white sleeve stripes points at a CRT monitor; in the center foreground, another student with short spiky hair wears an oversized gray sweatshirt and sits facing away from the camera; on the right foreground, a blonde student with a ponytail wears a light blue long-sleeve top with dark horizontal arm stripes and types at a keyboard; far right, another student with curly dark hair sits at a workstation. The monitors prominently display the ChatGPT interface, with the visible heading reading {argument name="screen title" default="ChatGPT"} and simple prompt text beneath it. The room has beige walls, drop ceiling tiles, and multiple motivational classroom posters: exactly 4 readable posters on the back wall saying {argument name="poster one" default="YOU CAN DO HARD THINGS"}, "BE KIND ONLINE", "THINK BEFORE YOU CLICK", and a larger poster titled "KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS" with a list beneath it. Include a bit of stone edging and dark greenery at lower left and a brown tiled floor. Lighting is soft natural daylight, slightly overcast, with muted colors, shallow depth of field, and a vintage editorial photography look. Composition should be vertical, full seated figure, straight-on, balanced, and quietly uncanny. Customize the main figure as {argument name="person" default="a middle-aged woman"}, the bird as {argument name="bird type" default="black crow"}, the dog breed as {argument name="dog type" default="small poodle mix"}, the dog ear color as {argument name="dog ear color" default="orange"}, and the outfit palette as {argument name="outfit colors" default="white and faded pink florals"}.

### No. 63: रेट्रो पिक्सेल पर्वत घाटी

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

हाफटोन कॉमिक शेडिंग के साथ एक जीवंत पिक्सेल आर्ट अल्पाइन परिदृश्य, जो रेट्रो गेम पृष्ठभूमि, दृश्य पोस्टर, या नॉस्टैल्जिक पर्यावरण कला के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A highly detailed retro pixel art landscape of a bright alpine valley in summer, composed like a classic side-scrolling video game background but shown as a wide scenic vista. In the foreground, a winding tan dirt path curves from the bottom center into the middle distance through dense wildflower meadows, with a small blue stream at the lower right bordered by gray rocks and lush grass. Count 2 large foreground rock clusters, 1 winding path, and 1 visible stream. Fill the meadows with colorful flowers in vivid purple, yellow, red, pink, and white, with especially tall purple flower spikes on the left foreground and dense mixed blossoms on both sides of the path. On the left and right midground, place thick stands of leafy green trees and dark pine trees, framing the open valley center. In the background, show a dramatic mountain range with exactly 7 visible peaks: 1 dominant tall snow-capped peak slightly right of center, 2 medium purple peaks to its left, 2 smaller snowy blue peaks in the far center distance, 1 smaller purple peak to the right, and 1 cropped rocky mountain edge at the far left. Use vibrant greens and purples as the main palette, with cool blue shadows and lavender mountain faces. Above, render a bright blue sky with large creamy white clouds, halftone-dot shading throughout the sky and mountains, subtle vintage comic print texture, visible dithering, and crisp sharp pixel edges. Add exactly 4 small flying bird silhouettes in the sky. The whole image should feel colorful, nostalgic, scenic, and richly layered, with heavy halftone comic shading, retro print grain, no text, no UI, no characters, and no buildings.
```

### No. 67: जापानी एआई मॉडल प्रिस्क्रिप्शन शीट

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

एक एआई मॉडल के लिए एक हास्यपूर्ण जापानी प्रिस्क्रिप्शन फॉर्म की यथार्थवादी ओवरहेड फोटो, जो आधिकारिक दिखने वाले पैरोडी दस्तावेज़ और मॉक कागजात बनाने के लिए उपयोगी है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
{

    "paper": {
      "size": "A4 portrait",
      "color": "white",

    },

      "count": 6,
      "items": [
        { "label": "患者名", "value": "{argument name=\"patient name\" default=\"ChatGPT\"}" },
        { "label": "性別", "value": "N/A" },
        { "label": "年齢", "value": "N/A" },
        { "label": "モデル名", "value": "{argument name=\"model name\" default=\"GPT-5.4 Thinking\"}" }

      ]
    },

      "label": "備考",
      "text": "継続的な評価とフィードバックにより、モデルの健全性を維持すること。"
    },
    "footer_fields": {
      "count": 4,
      "items": [
        { "label": "医師名", "value": "{argument name=\"doctor name\" default=\"サム・アルトマン\"}" },
        { "label": "医療機関名", "value": "{argument name=\"institution name\" default=\"OpenAI\"}" }
      ]
    },
    "seal": {
      "position": "bottom right inside the form",
      "shape": "rounded rectangular red stamp box",
      "text_lines": 3,
      "text": ["OpenAI", "代表取締役", "サム・アルトマン"]
    },
    "disclaimer": "※この処方箋は非実在のモデルに対する診断・治療を目的としたものです。"
  },
  "layout": {
    "camera_angle": "top-down overhead",
    "framing": "entire sheet visible with narrow margins of wooden desk around it",
    "lighting": "soft indoor ambient lighting, even illumination, mild shadowing near paper edges",

### No. 68: चैटजीपीटी मज़ाकिया प्रिस्क्रिप्शन सेट

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

चैटजीपीटी के लिए एक मज़ाकिया जापानी मेडिकल प्रिस्क्रिप्शन और दवा सेट की यथार्थवादी ओवरहेड तस्वीर, जो पैरोडी स्वास्थ्य-थीम वाली प्रॉप ग्राफिक्स या सोशल मीडिया कॉन्सेप्ट आर्ट के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A realistic overhead product photograph on a warm wooden tabletop showing 6 medical-style items neatly arranged in two rows, designed as a humorous Japanese pharmacy set for ChatGPT. Bottom row: 2 blister packs of tablets and 1 small transparent zip bag of white powder, each aligned beneath the corresponding envelope. Dosage lines indicate twice daily after morning and evening meals, 1 tablet each time, for 7 days. Medicine box title: "【おくすり】" and drug name "幻覚抑制錠 5mg" with a smaller note saying it improves hallucinatory tendencies. Date also "2025年6月5日". Same clinic footer and blue medical cross icon.

Medicine box title: "【おくすり】" and drug name "プロンプト調整散 1g" with a smaller note saying it adjusts overfitting and prompt confusion. Date "2025年6月5日". Same clinic footer and blue medical cross icon.

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

एक काल्पनिक स्ट्रीटवियर और नेचुरल-वाइन ब्रांड के लिए छह-छवि एडिटोरियल फैशन अवधारणा दिखाता हुआ एक स्क्रीनशॉट-शैली वाला एआई मूडबोर्ड, जो कला निर्देशन डेक या अभियान संदर्भ बोर्डों को पुनर्निर्मित करने के लिए उपयोगी है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
Create a 4:5 editorial fashion lookbook moodboard for a fictional brand called {argument name="brand name" default="VINCO"}. The image is a dark-interface screenshot-style composition with a large rounded charcoal text panel across the upper half and a 2-by-3 grid of six fashion/editorial images in the lower left quadrant. The overall aesthetic blends Italian archival graphic design with late-1990s Southern California streetwear, mixing natural wine culture, skate utility, and sun-faded documentary fashion photography. Use gritty but precise art direction, midday outdoor light, slightly chaotic but disciplined typography, and real-person casting rather than polished fashion-model energy. In the image grid, include exactly 6 tiles: tile 1 shows a young man in an oversized faded olive T-shirt and dark pants standing in front of an off-white poster-like backdrop with bold {argument name="logo text" default="VINCO"} branding, barcode graphics, and small editorial text; tile 2 is a close-up still life of a dark wine bottle with a minimalist white label reading {argument name="bottle label" default="VINCO"}, photographed in warm sunlight with tactile paper texture and shadow; tile 3 shows a person from the back in a washed olive long-sleeve shirt with large subtle chest or back branding, white shorts, and a yellow hanging tag or sticker element near the top right, posed against a pale wall with blue stripe detail and editorial layout text; tile 4 shows a skateboarder crouching or riding away, photographed from behind, wearing a white T-shirt with a large black graphic block on the back and dark shorts, in golden sun on pavement; tile 5 is a printed wine ephemera flat lay with cream paper and a pale chartreuse-green wine label or booklet reading {argument name="product text" default="Vino Naturale"}, featuring grape illustration, small black text, and layered paper pieces; tile 6 shows a person facing camera in a white T-shirt with a race-bib style chest print reading 97, wearing a fluorescent yellow-green cap with small brand text, standing outdoors with palm trees and bright sky behind them. Keep the six images slightly imperfect and collage-like, as if pulled from a campaign deck or saved references. Use earthy tones throughout: olive, cream, charcoal, sun-bleached white, asphalt gray, muted brown, and one fluorescent yellow-green accent repeated in small details. Include visible interface framing around the composition: a dark app-like background, the lower image grid aligned left, and a rounded gray “Edit” button near the bottom left, plus a small circular icon near the bottom right, reinforcing that this is a screenshot of a generated moodboard rather than a clean standalone poster.
```

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

At the lower left, include 1 old-fashioned streetlamp and a dense cluster of blooming hydrangeas in blue and violet along a stone wall. The town below is packed with tiled rooftops, narrow streets, warm window lights, and layered houses, with distant mountains framing the bay. Use dramatic rim light, luminous atmospheric perspective, sparkling highlights, delicate cloud detail, and emotional, nostalgic color grading in indigo, ultramarine, pink, peach, and gold. Design it explicitly as a Japanese animated film poster with elegant typography integrated into the artwork: large hand-brushed Japanese title text across the upper-left to center reading {argument name="title text" default="星をつなぐ約束のうた"}, smaller English subtitle beneath it reading {argument name="English subtitle" default="The Song of Promises"}, a small award-laurel line in Japanese at the top left, 1 vertical Japanese tagline along the upper-right edge, 4 cast names in Japanese centered near the bottom, a release date at the lower left reading {argument name="release date" default="8.23"} with "ROADSHOW" below, 1 pink Japanese tagline across the lower center, and a website/social handle at the lower right. ![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

In the bay, include exactly 3 traditional Maltese fishing boats in vivid blue, yellow, red, and green, plus 2 tiny white sailboats farther back. Add exactly 4 white seagulls flying across a brilliant turquoise-blue sky with soft white clouds. Frame the whole composition with dark leafy trees and abundant bright magenta bougainvillea blossoms arching in from the top and right edges, with more flowers in the lower right corner, creating a lush border around the scene. Include a palm tree among the waterfront buildings and a spiky agave plant in the lower left foreground. यह प्रॉम्प्ट पक्षियों और जानवरों से घिरे एक मास्कधारी धनुर्धर का स्वप्निल सिनेमाई फैशन-शैली का चित्र बनाता है, जो अलौकिक संपादकीय या ललित कला छवि निर्माण के लिए उपयोगी है।

Add 1 red-headed crane-like bird at the far right edge, visible in profile. The image should feel dreamlike, strange, and symbolic rather than realistic, with crisp midday sunlight, rich saturated colors, soft film grain, and a slightly vintage editorial-photography look. Use low-angle perspective, dynamic diagonal lines from the bow and arrow, and layered animal placement to create tension and motion. Dry grasses appear at the bottom edge, but the background is mostly open sky. Highly detailed fabric folds, natural bird wing positions, and a balanced surreal composition.

### No. 105: ऐतिहासिक आविष्कार समयरेखा ग्रिड

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट इतिहास भर में लेबल किए गए आविष्कार डायोरामा के ग्रिड को दर्शाता हुआ एक चर्मपत्र-शैली वाला शैक्षिक पोस्टर उत्पन्न करता है, जो समयरेखा इन्फोग्राफिक्स और दुनिया बदलने वाली प्रौद्योगिकी तुलना के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
Create a square infographic-style illustration showing a {argument name="grid size" default="15×15"} invention timeline grid rendered as a collection of miniature isometric dioramas on aged parchment tiles. The image should look like a curated historical poster that spans from {argument name="starting year" default="1000 BC"} to {argument name="ending year" default="2026"}, with one invention per tile and no repeats. Show the visible portion as a 5 by 5 section of the larger grid, for a total of 25 labeled tiles, arranged in neat rows and columns with thin dark borders. Every tile contains a unique world-changing invention depicted as a small handcrafted diorama with era-appropriate materials, colors, and background details. Use a warm antiquarian palette for ancient and medieval inventions, sepia technical-document tones for early modern inventions, and cooler neon-blue futuristic lighting for modern digital and biotech inventions. Surround the grid with an old-map border and subtle historical cartography textures, blending into faint modern network graphics near the bottom right.

Label each visible tile with a small beige caption tag in bold black text. Include exactly these 25 visible inventions in reading order from top left to bottom right: 1) {argument name="first tile label" default="1000 BC"} tile showing an iron plow and simple hand tools in a farm field, captioned "Iron Plow & Tools"; 2) "Concept of Zero" shown as a parchment-like tile with a carved zero symbol and a blue hourglass; 3) "Water Clock" shown as a wooden water-timing device; 4) "Catapult" shown as a wooden siege engine; 5) "Antikythera Mechanism" shown as an intricate bronze gear device in a stone niche; 6) "Concrete" shown as a wheelbarrow filled with wet cement or mortar; 7) "Wheelbarrow" shown as a simple wooden one-wheel cart; 8) "Windmill" shown as a traditional mill on grassy ground; 9) "Gunpowder" shown as a barrel and a mound of black powder with smoke; 10) "Printing Press" shown as a wooden press framed by classical columns; 11) "Mechanical Clock" shown as an ornate standing clock; 12) "Telescope" shown as an early brass telescope on a tripod with sketch-like scientific notes; 13) "Steam Engine" shown on a blue blueprint-style tile with an early locomotive engine; 14) "Electric Battery" shown on a blueprint-like tile with two cylindrical battery cells and wiring; 15) "Telegraph" shown as a Morse telegraph key on technical paper; 16) "Light Bulb" shown glowing warmly on a neutral pedestal; 17) "Automobile" shown as an early red motorcar on a workshop-plan background; 18) "Airplane" shown as a commercial jet aircraft in miniature; 19) "Transistor" shown as a black microchip on a luminous circuit-board tile; 20) "Personal Computer" shown as a beige desktop computer with CRT monitor and keyboard; 21) "World Wide Web" shown as a glowing blue globe over digital circuitry; 22) "Smartphone" shown as a sleek modern phone on a neon-tech background; 23) "CRISPR-Cas9" shown as a DNA double helix in a biotech-blue display tile; 24) "Reusable Rocket" shown as several upright rockets launching with exhaust clouds; 25) "AI (LLMs)" shown as glowing large letters AI in a holographic tech cube; 26) "Brain-Computer Interface" shown as a glowing brain hologram on a blue platform; 27) "Advanced Neural Interface (Implant)" shown as a transparent human head profile with a glowing brain implant, with a small top label reading "2026".

Keep the composition highly organized, poster-like, and visually dense, with each tile readable at a glance. Use slight isometric perspective, crisp linework, painterly shading, and polished editorial illustration quality. The overall feeling should combine museum poster, educational timeline, and imaginative historical-tech diorama art.
```

```
A top-down cinematic still life of a vintage classified investigation dossier on a dark wooden desk, centered and filling most of the frame. The top folder is the main focus and is clipped at the upper left with 1 oversized silver paper clip. Across the top center, typewritten in bold black monospaced letters, the headline reads {argument name="headline text" default="CONFIDENTIAL – CASE FILES"}, with a thin horizontal rule beneath it. On the right edge of the folder stack, show 1 tabbed side label reading "CASE FILE NO." with a thick black redaction bar below it. Include 5 numbered sections exactly: "1. SUBJECT INFORMATION", "2. CASE SUMMARY", "3. DETAILS", "4. ASSOCIATES / CONTACTS", and "5. REMARKS". In the header area, include the fields "CASE FILE NO.:" with a black redaction bar, "DATE OPENED:" with {argument name="date opened" default="March 14, 20___"}, "PREPARED BY:" with a black redaction bar, "DEPARTMENT:" with {argument name="department" default="Internal Investigations Unit"}, and "CLASSIFICATION:" with {argument name="classification" default="CONFIDENTIAL"}. In section 3, add a second paragraph of details text with 4 separate black redaction bars embedded in the paragraph. In section 5, add a short warning sentence about sensitive information and unauthorized disclosure. Use warm sepia lighting, soft shadows around the folder edges, subtle vignetting, and a moody noir archival atmosphere. The image should feel realistic, tactile, secretive, and slightly dusty, like a confidential detective case file photographed for a crime thriller or worldbuilding prop.

### No. 110: चनक्कले का टाइनी प्लैनेट एरियल दृश्य

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

यह प्रॉम्प्ट चनक्कले के वाटरफ्रंट लैंडमार्क्स का यथार्थवादी 360-डिग्री टाइनी-प्लैनेट ड्रोन दृश्य बनाता है, जो ट्रैवल इमेजरी और सिटी-पोस्टर विज़ुअल्स के लिए आदर्श है।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A dramatic ultra-wide aerial tiny-planet photograph of {argument name="city name" default="Canakkale"}, Turkey, rendered as a full 360-degree stereographic projection so the city and waterfront form a compact spherical world surrounded by a swirling ring of blue sky and white clouds. The viewpoint is high above the shoreline in bright daytime with crisp summer light, realistic colors, and strong photographic detail. Place the large hillside sign reading {argument name="landmark sign text" default="Canakkale"} prominently across the center of the miniature planet. On the left-upper side of the sphere, show a tall pale stone clock tower with a small red Turkish flag at the top, surrounded by dense urban blocks with red-tiled roofs and mid-rise buildings. On the right side, include a vivid blue harbor with 2 white passenger ferries docked along the waterfront and a long curving coastline extending into the distance. In the lower-right quadrant, feature the monumental dark wooden Trojan horse statue on a circular plaza. In the lower-left quadrant, include the large rectangular concrete memorial structure set within green parkland. Cover the planet with winding pedestrian paths, lawns, trees, and landscaped gardens, with city streets and waterfront promenades visible around the edges. Use a highly realistic drone-photo look, deep depth of field, sharp textures, slightly exaggerated fisheye distortion from the tiny-planet projection, and a majestic travel-poster composition emphasizing the contrast between the green park, historic landmarks, and sparkling sea.
```

### No. 111: अस्वाभाविक फुल-बॉडी एलियन पोर्ट्रेट

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

कृत्रिम प्राणी अवधारणा कला, साइ-फाई की आर्ट, या बेचैन कर देने वाले मॉडल क्षमता प्रदर्शन के लिए उपयुक्त, एक दुबले-पतले ह्यूमनॉइड एलियन की एक अंधेरी फोटोरियलिस्टिक स्टूडियो छवि।

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A hyper-realistic full-body studio portrait of a disturbing humanoid alien standing alone against a dark, smoky blue-black backdrop. The creature is extremely tall and emaciated, with elongated limbs, a narrow waist, long thin fingers, and oversized bare feet planted on a dim studio floor. Its skin is smooth but leathery and subtly wrinkled, colored deep charcoal blue with cold gray highlights, showing sharply defined ribs, sternum, collarbones, tendons, and stringy musculature across the chest, abdomen, shoulders, and neck. The torso is hairless and gaunt, with an eerie anatomical realism that feels biologically plausible but unsettling. The head is bald, enlarged, and slightly bulbous with a classic extraterrestrial silhouette, attached to an unnaturally long neck; keep the face obscure, unreadable, and deeply uncanny rather than expressive. Pose the alien front-facing with a slight three-quarter angle, arms hanging loosely at its sides, posture upright but subtly predatory, centered in frame from head to feet. Use low-key cinematic lighting with a faint cool rim light and soft overhead illumination that sculpts every crease and contour while keeping the overall scene dark, moody, and oppressive. Desaturated palette, ultra-detailed skin texture, photoreal creature design, sharp focus, high contrast, ominous atmosphere, no clothing, no props, no environment details beyond the shadowy studio background.
```

यह प्रॉम्प्ट एक निराशाजनक चट्टानी घाटी में एक यथार्थवादी ह्यूमनॉइड एलियन का एक विचलित कर देने वाला फुल-बॉडी साइ-फाई हॉरर पोर्ट्रेट उत्पन्न करता है, जो सिनेमाई अवधारणा कला और कृत्रिम प्राणी डिजाइन के लिए आदर्श है।

A full-body cinematic portrait of a deeply unsettling humanoid alien standing alone in a dark rocky ravine, centered in the frame and facing forward in a neutral upright pose with both arms hanging low at its sides. The creature is extremely tall and emaciated, with elongated limbs, narrow shoulders, a sunken torso, visible rib-like structures, taut sinewy anatomy, long forearms, oversized hands with long thin fingers, and long digitigrade-looking feet planted on wet black ground. The neck and upper chest are fused into a disturbing organic structure, with tendril-like folds and open channels running from the clavicle area upward into the head. The head is broad and mushroom- or hammer-shaped with a ridged crown and flared side lobes, giving a nonhuman silhouette; the face should feel unreadable and alien rather than cute or familiar. Place the figure in a narrow canyon of dark eroded stone, with 2 large foreground rock masses framing the subject on the left and right, and a misty cliff wall receding behind it. Use cold desaturated lighting, soft fog, damp surfaces, shallow atmospheric haze, and a grim monochrome palette of charcoal, slate, ash gray, and muted flesh tones. The mood should be uncanny, realistic, oppressive, and biologically plausible, like a high-end sci-fi horror still. Ultra-detailed photorealism, sharp texture on the creature, subtle depth of field, dramatic natural backlight from above, no clothing, no tools, no background creatures, no gore, no text.

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

This prompt generates a fully typeset Japanese fantasy anime film poster featuring a silver-haired moon-themed heroine, ideal for cinematic key art and promotional poster concepts.

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A dramatic Japanese fantasy anime movie poster, vertical one-sheet composition, centered on a beautiful teenage girl with very long flowing silver-white hair, glowing golden eyes, and a calm inviting smile, reaching one hand toward the viewer. She wears a black-and-white celestial dress with a fitted corset bodice, white chest panel, black ribbon lacing at the front, detached black sleeves with soft white ruffles, a black belt at the waist, layered skirt panels decorated with exactly 3 gold crescent moon ornaments, and a black choker with a gold crescent moon pendant. She also has exactly 1 gold crescent moon hair clip near her bangs. Behind her is a luminous night sky filled with stars, nebula-like clouds, and a huge eclipsed moon halo directly above her head, plus exactly 3 floating crescent-ring light effects around the left side of her hair. The background shows an ornate fantasy city with towering gothic palace architecture, spires, observatory-like structures, and glowing windows, all bathed in cool moonlight. Use a rich palette of deep indigo, violet, midnight blue, silver, and gold, with sparkles, magical particles, rim lighting, glossy highlights, and a slightly dense, painterly modern-anime poster finish.

Design it as a fully typeset Japanese film poster with elegant serif display typography in gold and white. At the very top, place a centered headline in Japanese: {argument name="headline text" default="夜が欠けるたび、忘れていた真実が目を覚ます。"}. On the right side, set a large vertical Japanese tagline in gold: {argument name="right-side tagline" default="最後の月光が消える前に、世界の記憶をつなぎ直せ。"}. On the left side, arrange 4 stacked blocks of smaller Japanese body copy separated by decorative divider lines and crescent motifs. Add a circular gold burst badge on the lower right with Japanese promotional text inside. Across the lower middle, place the large glowing Japanese title in ornate gold-white lettering: {argument name="movie title" default="月蝕のリグレット"}. Beneath the title, add a smaller centered Japanese subtitle line. Below that, place a horizontal feature line with exactly 3 gold-separated phrases in Japanese: "記憶", "月光", "観測魔法". At the very bottom, add 3 short Japanese teaser lines spread left, center, and right, and a large glowing release line centered under them: {argument name="release text" default="近日公開"}. The overall feeling is epic, melancholic, magical, celestial, romantic, and nostalgic, like a high-budget fantasy anime film poster.

### No. 117: Dark Fantasy Cliffside Outpost

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)

#### 📖 विवरण

This prompt generates a moody dark-fantasy landscape painting of a ruined encampment on a cliff, ideal for worldbuilding art, RPG settings, or ominous book-cover style scenes.

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A dark fantasy matte painting of a bleak hilltop encampment overlooking a vast cursed wasteland at dusk. In the left foreground, a ragged hanging banner reads "The Pale Lodge Outpost" in large black hand-painted letters, attached to wooden poles and weathered by wind. Beside it stands a tall carved totem post topped with a black raven and draped with bones, skulls, and tattered ornaments. The camp itself contains 4 visible canvas tents: 2 large central tents, 1 medium tent on the left, and 1 smaller tent on the right, all in dirty beige fabric with black occult sigils painted on them, held by ropes, spikes, and crooked poles. Around the tents are 5 hooded human figures in dark robes, standing still like sentries or cultists. Near the center-left is a small campfire casting a faint orange glow. In the right foreground sit 2 brass-and-iron astronomical or ritual instruments on stone pedestals, resembling armillary spheres or astrolabes. The ground is uneven black rock at the edge of a cliff, with scattered stakes, lanterns, banners, and ritual posts. Beyond the outpost stretches a desolate valley of ash-colored plains, winding pale waterways, jagged rock spires, and distant mountain silhouettes. On the horizon, slightly right of center, a sinister dark castle rises from a lone hill. The sky is filled with enormous turbulent storm clouds, with 3 flying creatures or birds silhouetted in the distance and a break in the clouds casting cold, sickly light across the landscape. Use a grim, painterly, highly detailed style with muted sepia, charcoal, umber, and gray tones, dramatic atmospheric perspective, cinematic composition, and the mood of a foreboding fantasy frontier outpost at the edge of a dead world.
```

- **प्रकाशित:** 22 अप्रैल 2026
- **भाषाएं:** HI-IN

### No. 118: Epic Senna vs Prost Gladiator Poster

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

A dramatic vintage-style motorsport poster depicting Senna and Prost as mythic gladiator rivals, ideal for recreating cinematic tribute art or high-impact F1 legend posters.

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
An epic cinematic poster in a dark golden bronze palette, styled like a mythic gladiator movie poster merged with vintage Formula 1 iconography. Two legendary rival drivers face away from each other in mirrored side-profile bust portraits at the top half of the image, one on the left inspired by Ayrton Senna and one on the right inspired by Alain Prost, both depicted as heroic Roman gladiators with weathered bronze armor, dramatic shoulder plates, and racing colors draped as cloaks. The left figure wears green, yellow, and blue accents, and the right figure wears blue, white, and red accents. Their faces are mostly in shadow, lit by intense backlight through storm clouds, creating a solemn, monumental mood. Behind each driver hangs 1 vertical banner, for a total of 2 banners: the left banner is dark green with a large gold S, the text "SENNA", "#12", and a cursive signature; the right banner is dark blue with a large gold P, the text "PROST", "#1", and a cursive signature. Centered near the top, in elegant serif French text, place the line "DEUX LÉGENDES. UN SEUL TRÔNE." with a small gold Formula 1 emblem and laurel motif below it. In the central sky, add 2 stacked lines of French text reading "RIVAUX SUR LA PISTE." and "LÉGENDES POUR TOUJOURS." The main title dominates the middle in huge metallic serif lettering: "{argument name="headline text" default="SENNA vs PROST"}", with a sword-like vertical separator for "vs". Beneath it, a subtitle in French reads "LE COMBAT ULTIME DE LA F1". The lower half shows a colossal Roman colosseum packed with spectators, flags, arches, dust, smoke, and dramatic perspective lines converging on the center. At the exact center of the arena stands 1 large victory banner with the words "VICTOIRE GLOIRE HONNEUR" in gold. In the foreground, place 2 front-facing late-1980s Formula 1 cars charging toward the viewer on a dirt-covered arena floor, throwing dust. The left car is associated with Senna and features red-and-white Marlboro-inspired livery, Shell branding, and the number 12 on the nose, with the driver wearing a yellow helmet. The right car is associated with Prost and features matching red-and-white Marlboro-inspired livery, Shell branding, and the number 1 on the nose, with the driver wearing a white helmet. At the very bottom, add the line "1988. 1989. 1990." and below it "L’HISTOIRE S’ÉCRIT À PLUS DE 300 KM/H." Include a small ornamental laurel decoration under the final line. Use hyper-detailed textures, dramatic storm clouds, god rays, flying dust, intense contrast, symmetrical composition, ultra-polished poster design, heroic scale, and a timeless legendary atmosphere.
```

#### 🖼️ उत्पन्न चित्र

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://static.atlascloud.ai/prompt/gpt-image2/images/14610_1.jpg" width="600" alt="Epic Senna vs Prost Gladiator Poster - Image 1">
</div>

- **लेखक:** [nazca alwave](https://x.com/AlwaveNazca)
- **स्रोत:** [Twitter Post](https://x.com/AlwaveNazca/status/2046696943666024518#reversed-0)

### No. 119: Studio Portrait With Strawberry Ice Cream

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

This prompt generates a sleek celebrity-style studio portrait of a dark-haired woman holding a strawberry ice cream cone in front of her face, ideal for editorial beauty or pop-culture imagery.

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A polished studio portrait of a glamorous pop-star-like woman from the chest up, centered against a smooth neutral gray backdrop. She has {argument name="hair color" default="jet black"} long loose wavy hair with a middle part, glossy shine, and soft volume falling over both shoulders. Her face is mostly hidden behind the ice cream cone she is holding up in front of her mouth and lower face, creating a playful fashion-editorial composition. She wears a white ribbed tank top with wide straps and a single visible sparkling stud earring. In her hand is 1 waffle cone topped with 1 large scoop of pink strawberry ice cream with dark red berry swirls and slight melting texture. Warm, flattering beauty lighting, soft shadows, realistic skin tones, high-end celebrity portrait photography, crisp focus on the hand, cone, hair, and shoulders, minimal background, subtly sensual and chic mood, vertical crop.
```

### No. 120: Storm Wizard Casting Lightning

![Language-HI-IN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-HI-IN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 विवरण

A cinematic photorealistic fantasy prompt for generating a dramatic wizard portrait with storm lighting and crackling magical energy.

#### 📝 प्रॉम्पट

```
A dramatic dark-fantasy portrait of an elderly wizard standing in a stormy wasteland under a black, cloud-choked sky. He wears a tall, weathered pointed hat with a brown leather band and a tiny metal clasp, and a heavy dark blue-gray robe with wide sleeves. His face is mostly hidden in shadow beneath the hat brim, with long strands of glowing {argument name="accent hair color" default="electric blue"} hair peeking out at the sides and a very long flowing silver-white beard reaching down his chest. The wizard thrusts his left hand toward the camera in a powerful forced-perspective pose, fingers spread, conjuring a bright orb of blue-white magical energy in his palm with crackling lightning arcs wrapping around the hand and sleeve. In his right arm he clutches a large ancient leather spellbook with worn corners, metal fittings, embossed arcane markings on the cover, and a few pages visible. The background shows a barren dark landscape and exactly 1 prominent lightning bolt striking on the right side of the frame. Cinematic high-contrast lighting, hyper-detailed skin and fabric texture, moody photorealism, sharp focus on the hand and beard, intense fantasy atmosphere, centered composition, square crop.
```

## 🤝 योगदान कैसे करें

हम योगदान का स्वागत करते हैं! आप निम्नलिखित तरीकों से प्रॉम्पट्स जमा कर सकते हैं:

### 🐛 GitHub Issue

1. Click [**नया प्रॉम्पट जमा करें**](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts/issues/new?template=prompt.yml)
2. प्रॉम्पट विवरण और छवि के साथ फॉर्म भरें
3. जमा करें और टीम समीक्षा की प्रतीक्षा करें
4. यदि अनुमोदित (हम `approved` लेबल जोड़ेंगे), तो यह स्वचालित रूप से CMS के साथ सिंक हो जाएगा
5. आपका प्रॉम्पट 4 घंटे के भीतर README में दिखाई देगा

**नोट:** गुणवत्ता नियंत्रण सुनिश्चित करने के लिए हम केवल GitHub Issues के माध्यम से जमा स्वीकार करते हैं।

विस्तृत दिशानिर्देशों के लिए [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) देखें।
